padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2254801">thispillthings</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-17">11/17/24 13:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Thé Noir 29 holds a special place in my so far compact collection—it was my first niche fragrance, and what an introduction it was. I bought a full bottle last October at Le Labo’s Berlin store, and the experience was unforgettable: the cozy vibe of the store, and the care they put into everything.<br />
<br />
As for the scent? Pure magic. It’s a deep tea, smoky fig and just the right amount of musk. The contrast between its dried-fruity notes and the darker, woody base feels timeless yet modern. There’s a cool, laid-back elegance to it.<br />
<br />
Comment under that states it could be overwhelming leaves me clueless. Thé Noir is not loud, it’s the kind of fragrance that draws people in close, making them wonder what smells so good. <br />
I wore it to the office and basically everywhere for 6 months truth be told I’m an undersprayer. For anyone new to niche (me), I think this is the perfect gateway scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2352214"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2352214#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2350950" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1857053">thewho</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-11">11/11/24 18:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Noir 29 by Le Labo 3/5<br />
<br />
First impression is stale black pepper. It is very earthy like pu'er tea. Maybe it's the fig note which I'm learning that I dislike in perfumery. It is a subtle scent that becomes a skin scent within five minutes but I do get whiffs of it throughout a four hour time frame. Lasted on my clothes for days. It is not blind buy safe. Wish the bergamot was more prominent. Almost gives me old musty library in the fall vibes in the best way. Not the way that I want to smell, but could be perfect for someone else. <br />
<br />
Purchased a discovery set of 5mL travel bottles from the San Jose store. Wore at home. Would not repurchase.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2345835"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2345835#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2340333" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2340333" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jaylopez2024"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139090"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2139090.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jaylopez2024" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2340333ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2340333" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139090">Jaylopez2024</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-06">11/06/24 19:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>very oen Personal Review: Le Labo The Noir 29 Perfume<br />
<br />
Le Labo's The Noir 29 is a fragrance that captivates with its initial burst of rich, earthy notes. The blend of fig, bay leaves, and cedar creates a warm and alluring aroma that feels sophisticated and unique. It's a scent that draws compliments and sparks curiosity, making it a great choice for both casual and formal occasions.<br />
<br />
However, I did notice that it tends to transform into a skin scent rather quickly on me—within just an hour, the vibrant notes fade significantly. While the lingering scent is still pleasant, I find myself wishing for more longevity. The initial experience is delightful, but the fading leaves me wanting more of that captivating aroma throughout the day.<br />
<br />
Overall, The Noir 29 is a fantastic fragrance with a great smell, but if you're looking for something that lasts, you may want to consider layering it or reapplying for a longer-lasting experience. It’s definitely worth trying, especially if you appreciate its unique profile!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2340333"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2340333#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2339095" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="lmatt4122"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2286132"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2286132.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="lmatt4122" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Orto-Parisi/Brutus-24194.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.24194.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Brutus"title="Brutus"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2339095ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2339095" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2286132">lmatt4122</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-05">11/05/24 13:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is such a memorable fragrance, and the biggest compliment getter in my collection. The top notes perfectly mix the gourmand of fig with the juicy citrus of bergamot, yet the dry spice of the bay leaf restraints the opening from being overly sweet. The woodsy, musky middle and base notes flourish around the the fig and bergamot almost as if to present you with the distant, hazy memory of a summer day, as recorded in your journal over a cup of hot tea. It is romantic, melancholic, poetic. <br />
<br />
The performance is decent. I can usually smell it on my clothes the next day. I have received compliments from strangers over an arms length away. This is a people pleaser. One downside is that many of my friends also have this fragrance, so it has lost some of its aura. Still, I love it and wear it all the time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2339095"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2339095#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2339066" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2339066" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="charlotte__"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1354164"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1354164.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="charlotte__" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2339066ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2339066" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1354164">charlotte__</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-05">11/05/24 12:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is a beautiful resort hotel on Playa Riviera in Mexico that I recently travelled to for a spa week. It is a new build, the indoor outdoor kind with balcony bathtubs and travertine floors and overflowing lush plant pots. The hotel uses this scent in their hallways, wooden shutters that over look the infinity pools and let in a balmy gulf coast breeze. This is what it smells like. Black tea with a faint spice of wood that is incredibly indulgent and elegant. It is a true hotel scent. But I’m surprised no one has pointed out the beautiful stickiness of honey that seems to linger at the top notes. This fragrance is impossibly chic. It does not yell for attention but it draws people in its effortless quiet luxury. Perfect in the tacky humidity of summer. Day to Night.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2339066"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2339066#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2333918" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2333918" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="darkforestmags"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1170902"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1170902.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="darkforestmags" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.64757.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bianco Latte"title="Bianco Latte"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2333918ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2333918" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1170902">darkforestmags</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-31">10/31/24 16:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Trialing this on the third rainy autumn day in a row and I can’t think of a better scent to be wearing than Noir 29. Tea fragrances to me can often pull rather thin, but Noir 29 has some meat on its bones, it’s full bodied. This opens with ripe fig and tea, along with something a bit fruity that I can’t identify, and is grounded by a lightly woody base that veers greener as it dries down. <br />
<br />
This is a rather slick fragrance, polished. There’s a little soapiness in there, it’s clean, but it’s unobtrusive. I anticipated it being a bit darker and/or stronger than it is but it’s friendly, I think, and imminently wearable. Becomes a little sweet in the dry down, but is rounded out by the (light) tobacco and cedar. Just a gorgeous fall/winter fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2333918"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2333918#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2331545" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; unfortunately I always amp the latter. I was thinking I might like it more on a man, but I agree with the reviewer describing it as more of a home scent. Kind of a funky, over-steeped herbal tea and maybe some fig perfume. After drydown, I find the musk note too rugged and not naturalistic enough, changing the feel for the worse. That's not to say it is an unpleasant scent; just not for me, but I am also unsure of what its identity is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2331545"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2331545#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2331298" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2204876">eusp</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-08">10/08/24 11:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought a 5ml sample expecting this to be adequately masculine for me, a 40 year old male. I love the scent, and the opening is predominantly fig (less sweet than Wild Fig and Cassis from Jo Malone) which fades away after 30 mins or so to a mostly cedar base. It smells like a wearable festive candle on dry down, so is definitely one to wear in autumn and winter.<br />
<br />
It's beautifully blended and delicious, but my wife and I agree that it's more feminine and that she'd be better off wearing it than me. I'm not sure on performance yet, it didn't seem to last that long on me (2 sprays around the neck - and one on each arm - lasted 3 hours tops) but it may last longer on a lady with less body hair or with more sprays.<br />
<br />
Edit: smells more linear on my wife and lasts longer too. I'll be buying her a bottle as I love the smell, just not on me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2309039"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2309039#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307695" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The fig in the opening is so pleasant and then gives way to that incredible cedar during the dry down. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1389884">derby2169</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-02">10/02/24 08:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Clean sweet fig and smoky woods<br />
<br />
The Noir is definitely pleasant, opening with fruit like raw material, fig-like but not as intensely green, more so nectarine like, with a slight herbal almost leathery element to it. Im reminded almost of a bit of a slightly smoky slightly waxy woody leather, which I assume was meant to be interpreted as vetiver and tobacco notes. To my nose it definitely makes me think more so of a snuffed out candle with elements of designer leather, a certain dry almost oxidized metallic facet in the back. <br />
I dont really get realistic black tea, the dry slightly herbal woody leathery elements do evoke it effectively though, but with ample sweetness cutting through. <br />
<br />
Pleasant to wear. Even the candle/wax elements feel fitting and pleasant. Probably wouldn't spend the money on it though as it isnt provoking the emotional response I expect at the price point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2302347"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2302347#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2301703" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; No, it doesn’t smell like lipstick from 1997- *to me* - as perfume is always subjective, as some seemingly have forgotten… <br />
And it definitely isn’t being praised by people who are being paid to do so and haven’t smelt it lol.<br />
I visited a store for a straight year just to spray it cos I became so in love and so addicted. Has granted me many compliments now that I have a full bottle that I received for my birthday. <br />
<br />
In my top 5 signature / HG scents- truly a beautiful, unique, multifaceted and addictive scent. I adore tea scents but I don’t necessarily pick that up as the most prominent facet. To me it smells like a ever so slightly fermented fig elixir, steeped with black tea, on a cold day overlooking a view, with a faint waft of woody smoke from the distance. <br />
Conversely, it is also dark and nighttime evoking, sexy but not in a overt way, moreso in a confident, unisex, intriguing way. <br />
<br />
Longevity and projection (as someone who has struggled with these factors chronically w fragrances) are stellar, into the next morning I can still smell it on my wrist. <br />
<br />
∞/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2262157"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2262157#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260680" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It opens with a gentle sweetness, light and airy, yet there's an underlying darkness that aligns with its name. <br />
The top notes reveal a slightly sweet fig, accompanied by floral hints like marigold, and a rich black tea note. As it settles, dry woods emerge, contributing a subtle tannic quality that persists throughout. <br />
<br />
The scent is expertly blended and remains fairly linear from start to finish. With excellent projection, it's a fragrance that I would confidently recommend as a safe blind buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2257213"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2257213#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2252240" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I’m immediately reminded of Witch Hazel) and boozy fig. BUT I can NEVER AGREE with this smelling SOUR. Neither on my skin or my clothes, most Le Labo scents I tried have no sour smell at all. <br />
<br />
This smells like black tea, rosewater, and tobacco. Those are the three dominant things I pick up throughout its life. It smells edgy and cool, I’d imagine someone wearing all black and suede, in a cool coffee shop in New York City or L.A. carrying around a Les Paul guitar wearing this. Certainly makes me feel a little gothic and punkish. Sounds about Le Labo.<br />
<br />
Projects for hours, cool aura for about half the day. Transforms into a narcotic, spicy smell that’s just amazing. Skin scent after the 9 hour mark.<br />
<br />
This and Patchouli 24 are probably the only Le Labo scents I’d go full bottle for, everything else just feels overpriced, derivative, and underwhelming. 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This one was a gift and unexpectedly opened up tea fragrances as a category for me. The scent smells sophisticated, very Brooklyn, but not too young and not classic/old school. Really love the tobacco and hay smokiness surrounding the tea note in it. Just wish it was less expensive.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2222250"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2222250#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2220096" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2220096" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="hugowasmyhomeboy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2196042"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="hugowasmyhomeboy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2220096ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2220096" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2196042">hugowasmyhomeboy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-16">07/16/24 07:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Interesting frag.<br />
I get rose and vetiver mostly, a "dirty rose"-kinda scent. There's a lurking muskiness reminiscent of the perfumes the old women in my life would wear, a red wine-ish note, and the citrus in the backdrop rounds it out. This flirts with the label old-fashioned, which I find quite endearing, but not everyone does. Eventually when you get deep into the drydown, the florals fade and there's a nice woody skin scent remaining.<br />
I'd say I'm impressed with it from a strict perfumery standpoint. Well-executed, great balance and not at all linear as it develops. Not loud. But I can't say I want to buy a full bottle either.<br />
I don't agree with the unisex label on here. Unisex to me implies equal consideration as a signature scent for both sexes; this has significantly more signature scent potential on the feminine side, whereas for most men it'll be a curiosity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It smells good on paper, got that woodsy, fig, subtle spice/sourness and ultimately a creaminess to it that feels dark but not midnight dark, more like a 6pm dim vibe that still has a touch of day wear / daylight to it but is ready for the evening, which is a great vibe to wear right as you wake up because who isn't ready for the day to be over - that's the overall vibe of the fragrance. It's not a bad sour, but the one commitment my collection of niche fragrances have is that no fragrance is a LOVE for me if it has a sourness to it (unless it's intentionally a citrus fragrance). It's got me divided down the middle on purchasing any bigger versions than the one that I have for this reason alone. For me, that's what makes this perfume a masterpiece. <br />
<br />
I made this my signature scent before I knew much about fragrance. I blind bought it after hearing someone gush about it and it's the only blind buy I haven't regretted. Even as my nose has matured and my research has expanded, I'm shocked to hear that this is a "tea scent" and many catch fig as the primary note. For me, there is little to no detectable fruit. It's bay leaf, hay, musk, and a whisper of citrus. It's gorgeous and relevant for almost every occasion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2183906"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2183906#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2183086" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2175625" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="babyflesh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2153287"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="babyflesh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Fantome/Vassago-83604.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.83604.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Vassago"title="Vassago"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2175625ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2175625" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2153287">babyflesh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-02">06/02/24 09:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love this fragrance because it's mature, but not at all grandma-ish or overtly sexy. I bought it a couple of years ago to celebrate turning 20, and its been the perfect early adulthood scent. It's the type of scent that feels perfect for casual outings and day-to-day life. It's hard to put it into words, but if you hate fresh/clean scents but wished you liked them, this might be for you. It's a snuggly, soft clean rather than a mountain spring clean. <br />
<br />
On my skin, the black tea definitely comes through strong, as does the fig. There's a nice soft powdery aspect to it as well. The wood and tobacco notes are very subtle, mostly just adding depth rather than standing out the way the tea and fig do. I don't notice the citrus much, but maybe that's just because its not very bright/tart.<br />
<br />
A really gorgeous scent overall. Maybe not a hot weather scent, but its very versatile.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2175625"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2175625#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174642" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1696314">Smokeandhoney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-02">05/02/24 02:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hugeeee dose of bergamot in the opening with a vegetal and green nuance, then becomes more fruity and figgy as time passes. The smoky tea element in this fragrance is very subtle and discreet, I wish I got more of that, sadly—perhaps if the vetiver and hay were more pronounced to my nose I’d get the desired effect. After that, a subdued fresh and ever so slightly syrupy rose peeps through which meddles nicely with the fig, then some soft woody touches. <br />
<br />
It really reminds me of a more fresh, sparkling and musky Pomegranate Noir from Jo Malone with more masculine leaning components coming from tobacco and cedar. I was expecting to smell something quite different to this but it is good, nonetheless.<br />
<br />
I tried 34 Blvd. St. Germain Eau de Toilette from Diptyque layered over the top of Thé Noir 29 and it was breathtaking.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2143012"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2143012#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2134490" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2074474">Ajlis</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-23">04/23/24 23:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume has perhaps the most enchanting opening note in the world. The aromas of black tea and cedar waft into my nose, dark and rich, making me breathe deeper and more calmly. Soon I also start to smell fig and rose among the woody tea scent. The combination is mystical, timeless and genderless, somehow nostalgic. No note dominates too much, but all are in perfect balance with each other. This is an atmospheric and meditative, deep and personal fragrance, one to wear for yourself. This may not garner compliments from all around you, but this is exactly what I would like to smell like when I walk alone in the city streets in a light drizzle on an autumn evening and wander into small antique shops to browse books. One of my all time favorite scents, I definitely want a bottle of this in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2134490"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2134490#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2131763" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1484705">salaryman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-12">04/12/24 18:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don’t think I’ve ever tried a fragrance with a fig note before so I wasn’t sure what to expect and if I’d even like it, especially seeing it combined with tobacco and hay. I thought it would be really strong, maybe even overwhelming, but all these notes come together and blend into a pleasant tea-like scent. The best way I’d describe Noir 29 is mature and comforting. It’s definitely something that fits my personal style, and I can see why it’s so popular!<br />
<br />
The Sillage is moderate at the beginning but quickly changes to sitting close to the skin. As certain notes fade away quicker than others the scent transforms into something more sour-y but not necessarily offensive. The longevity is long-lasting but for half of those hours the only thing you really smell is musk.<br />
<br />
This is the first one out of my set of testers that I’m wearing so I don’t know if I’ll buy a full bottle of this one just yet, but it’s definitely a strong opener!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1906122">ame87</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-10">04/10/24 13:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't know where to start with this one, when I smelled this at the shop, it was love at first sight, it was truly intoxicating, kept thinking about it everyday and put my intention on buying a 100 ml bottle after a month, a month passes and I buy the bottle, unfortunately, it barely lasts on me, the sillage is so intimate, even though I've seen already the reviews and it didn't seem that the performance was this bad, and I've smelled this perfume on others and it was amazing, so I assumed the sillage wasn't, boy was a I wrong, I am not sure whether it's my particular bottle or batch, I tried contacting customer service but they said they cannot do anything because I bought it from a third party authorised reseller, very disappointed, buy a 10ml decant before going for the whole thing. Won't buy this again unless they fix the longevity and sillage somehow</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2120590"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2120590#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2116575" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2116575" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ManicMonkey84"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1252174"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1252174.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ManicMonkey84" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Nest/Indigo-26845.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.26845.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Indigo"title="Indigo"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2116575ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2116575" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1252174">ManicMonkey84</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-06">04/06/24 15:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The best way I can describe this is black tea that comes across as both bright and a little dirty. There is a dry, incensey bitterness at the heart of the scent, but it's sheathed in a citric "juiciness" coming from the bergamot note. For me, the citrus and vetiver step forward more than the fig and tobacco, especially in the dry-down. It's a fairly gentle and flexible fragrance overall, probaly more suitable for warmer days when the sun is out. It stays pretty close to the skin, but doesn't really dissipate for a good 6+ hours on me. I understand people's gripe with Le Labo's inflated prices, but IMO The Noir 29 makes one of the better cases for its retail value.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Then over the years, the hype blew up and while I could see its appeal, I wondered what everyone was going wild over. <br />
<br />
Flash forward to this morning. My sister gave me a bunch of samples and I felt like wearing something generic while WFH so I gave myself a spritz...Holy heck! I'm transported right back to university at Stellenbosch, a summer afternoon, bag full of books and hanging out at the bar after lectures. And I've been floating in a happy little cloud since. <br />
<br />
Without stating the obvious note profile  (tea, underscored with fresh figs and balanced with dry hay) it brings to my mind sun-washed fields, which although summery, I can see it suiting any season. It's smart without being austere. Casual without sloppy. Pretty without being feminine. Just elegant, timeless and beautiful. Very signature-worthy.<br />
<br />
I wonder what I wasn't going wild over.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2104586"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2104586#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2096566" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; although definitely androgynous from the start, in the drydown it leans rather masculine</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2096125"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2096125#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2092396" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I have no business liking this: With all its woody, herbaceous, dry, sharp scent all up in my face.<br />
I would have been fine avoiding this, but some glorious creature I worked with breezed into the workplace with this on, and I couldn't help but harass her about it. She kept wearing each time we worked together, and - damn it all - it was spectacular.<br />
So, I assumed it would only work on her. All that unisex-leaning and individual skin chemistry, I thought I'd be safe.<br />
Until I bought my own sample.<br />
<br />
Now I have a (dupe) bottle and I spray it with wild abandon (coz I can't live among fragrance any other way).<br />
<br />
I can't even explain why it smells good. Usually I hate strong herbaceous scents, but - this does things to me. It smells amazing on clothes - Them little molecules love fabric.<br />
<br />
Cons, my Perfumites, include the following:<br />
 - Too expensive (I don't abide by the whole "But it's worth it" mentality; $AUD395/50ml and $AUD546/100ml for any perfume is despicable)<br />
 - Leans WILDLY masculine-dressed-up-as-unisex<br />
 - Maybe could use greater longevity?<br />
<br />
***<br />
<br />
Kitty rating: 9/10.<br />
<br />
~Compliment Counter~: 1 compliment: "Gosh, your perfume is so nice. I smelled it the entire time I've followed you"(Not as creepy as it sounds)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2085712"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2085712#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2084610" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It lives in the fridge and is a rare wear as I lean towards fesher musks these days -  but I love it.<br />
<br />
Overall: Dominating, spicy, cooling. <br />
<br />
It opens round and sour - like rice vinegar. There is a resinous cooling effect to the initial drydown. I get a little motor oil. <br />
<br />
As it shifts - dried fig and incense, spice. A little soapiness. <br />
<br />
At the end of the day- dusty, resinous wood, ozonic, cool leaves and soap. I can see how this might remind of Lapsang tea.<br />
<br />
What sets it apart: still get a clean freshness from it. Its smokey and resinous without being heavy or leathery.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2084258"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2084258#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2084124" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Getting a bottle</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2083342"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2083342#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2078723" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2039263">jckl</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-01">03/01/24 03:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A work of art - absolutely love this fragrance and has suddenly become my go-to<br />
<br />
Sweet through the fig but not enough to be sickening, smoky &amp; sophisticated with the black tea note, and dries down gorgeously on my skin (similar to the out-of-bottle scent). Personally, feel this leans a tiny bit masculine and a little towards colder weather, but brilliantly androgynous, mass-pleasing, and lasts all-day, even longer on clothes, scarves etc.<br />
<br />
Would also recommend trying a sample on skin, without comparing to other fragrances (difficult when sampling store, I know), as I originally hated the smokiness of this compared to Another 13 &amp; other of Le Labo's popular sellers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2078723"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2078723#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2073444" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2073444" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="einkill"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1876991"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1876991.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="einkill" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.31872.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Noir 29"title="The Noir 29"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2073444ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2073444" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1876991">einkill</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-25">02/25/24 05:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>with more longevity, this would be an ideal spring and summer scent of mine. it's androgynous and cozy, but not suffocating. it's dark and soft. it brought to life a scene with 木漏れ日 (komorebi), sitting under trees with books, paper and fountain pens, with sunlight dancing through the leaves and branches above. it reminds me of a cool breeze on quiet, warm, summer nights. or, walking through a forest as it is nearly dried after heavy rain.<br />
<br />
however... the aforementioned scenes wouldn't last long. beyond 20 minutes, i could smell little to nothing of Noir 29 left on me, like others have noted. not being a fan of gourmands and thus, fig notes, i wore this on days where i wanted whatever short time i could get with the vetiver and tobacco leaf notes. though the initial fig was too sweet, it slowly harmonised with the tobacco leaf and vetiver, when i could smell it. at it's dry down, the black tea notes are just barely hanging off my skin, and it's as if the fig and tobacco leaf were the only anchors for the black tea to be detectable. though, i really have to sit and sniff my arm for a minute to notice how the notes have settled. <br />
<br />
what took me by surprise was when my laboratory partner asked what i was wearing after 4 hours in lab, where her workstation was not quite close to me. hearing that she could smell it the entire time, was confusing. what she could smell, i couldn't. the black tea notes are just barely distinguishable from my skin. i'm not sure if this changes anything besides my sticking to 2-3 sprays. i might try using this as a hair scent to use up the sample. <br />
<br />
in the end, Noir 29 is like a cigarettes after sex song. atmospheric, androgynous, cozy, warm and dark, but with the feeling of there being something missing. so long as it's there, i'll come back to it. even if i'm not fully satiated by it; it's nice to just be adorned by it's existence, short as it may be.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2073444"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2073444#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2072557" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Later on I get some kind of rose even tough it is not listed? I see now that other also have commented on this, and it makes a lot of sense. I love the hay in the drydown tho! On my skin it feels like how I imagine the style boho chick smells like. Sometimes I get the tobacco note as well and it is lovely and complex and gives a great depht to the scent. The hay and the tobacco is what makes this bearable for me, and gives that oump to the green-ness. But my god this is so strong and it dominates almost the entire house if I spray more than two spritz. Be careful, but more importantly, enjoy!<br />
<br />

I feel like I can’t wear it a lot of the time because of that big cloud that follows you around, or maybe it’s because I’m not confident enough for it?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Citrus done in a deep, dark way. Not the usual light and airy citrus.<br />
The base in this is really centre stage. <br />
Heavy woodiness, vetiver and tobacco.<br />
<br />
There's something in here that's not sitting great on me.<br />
I can't quite put my finger on what it is; but, it's a thick, botanical/herbaceous, slightly medicinal ointment.<br />
It's not bad; I'm just getting a really thick wall of it. Which i'm finding overpowering.<br />
<br />
Luckily as it dries down, some of those more confrontational initial notes subside.<br />
Making way for a stale, musky tobacco.<br />
<br />
VERDICT:<br />
I would appreciate this more on others, not on myself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2052617"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2052617#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2052001" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; On the top edge there's a slightly sour bite from the citrus that adds a really interesting dimension. One of the most addicting dry downs I've come across with a balance of tobacco, tea, and musk. Not dry and dark like a woody scent, more of an herbal cedar accord. Amazing fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2049110"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2049110#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2048731" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I immediately felt it was in its own league. It makes me think of a wild night camping- the fire has nearly burned out and only little embers flicker. Perhaps it’s barely dawn, the grass is wet, and the birds are gently calling to each other. Sweet fig peaks through cool grey air as you roll a fresh cigarette, a mug of black tea steams atop a tree stump. Content and hazy, you sit with nature replaying the shenanigans from the night before. It’s very earthy. Very sexy. A bit hedonistic. Any gender can pull this off with the right energy. I’ve been avoiding Le Labo because of the price tag, but this does smell like it’s composed of the finest oils. <br />
<br />
I will say I go nose blind to this and that is not common for me. Just a heads up if you think it’s losing power fast, ask a friend if they can smell it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2028139"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2028139#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2023769" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Really, I did.  Fig, bay leaf, tobacco and tea are some of my favorite notes, so naturally this should be a winner, right?  Well, as it turns out, not exactly.  All those notes bastardize together so that my favorite scents become unrecognizable and transform The Noir 29 into something else entirely.<br />
<br />
Upon first spray, it smells like pine and Christmas.  So much so that I can’t imagine wearing this anytime other than winter – as if standing in a California forest of snow-covered cedar pine trees.  That holiday-hand-soap-scent remains pleasant but mildly cloying for hours, until the dry down modifies into a rotten aftershave scent that you want to scrub off immediately.<br />
<br />
In five words or less: Christmas present turned coal lump.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2021833"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2021833#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2021623" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Reminds me of a fine red wine - tannic and spicy, with little fruit or sourness on the nose. I can't find anything objectionable in TN29, unless one doesn't care for dark tea and rose notes at all. Performance is good, but not great for a niche edp. The excellent Dossier clone, a bit more fresh/less powdery, performs far better, with both greater projection and staying power. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-24">12/24/23 00:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Noir 29 is a rich, luxe, beautiful fragrance that has the best tea note I've ever smelled in my life, and I generally hate tea. The herbs, cedar, musk, hay, slight sweetness, and tobacco perfectly compliment the black tea note. Posh and stout fragrance with good performance, that smells like pure class. It feels substantial like the vibe of a patch or leather fragrance, but without those notes. The color really does feel Noir and if I didn't see the color of the juice, I'd expect it to be dark black. <br />
<br />
Extremely versatile, it feels at home formal, casual, day or night. I prefer it as a night out scent. I've only come across one other fragrance which is Murdock Black Tea the that smells like this.The Murdock is like a more diffusive cologne version of this one, that's got that same wonderful black tea note. <br />
<br />
-------------------------------------------<br />
Appealing to casual fragrance fans and niche aficionados alike. Smells deep, dark, expensive, and compliment factor is there if that's something you care about. This should be everyone's list to try and is bottle worthy IMO. <br />
<br />
Scent 9/10<br />
Performance 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="2009330"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=2009330#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2009038" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Smells of pencil shavings, ink, and of course, the cigars themselves. What a surprisingly nostalgic, dry, distinct impression. I consider Thé Noir a clean, intriguing  tobacco scent more than anything, of course I have my own deep-rooted associations to which this can be attributed. Calm, quiet, contemplative, clean in the same way as a wash in the ocean at night. The water is gentle, but one can’t help but feel cautious. I so love this subtle dissonance.<br />
<br />
Fig is present and pronounced at first, then settles into a soft and, for my tastes necessary sweetness in the background. I definitely get the tobacco, bay leaf, cedar, and hay the whole ride. Edit; somebody told me this smells like a beeswax and i cannot unsmell it rn</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1991197"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1991197#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1991168" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1991168" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tamun"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1448795"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1448795.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tamun" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1991168ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1991168" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1448795">tamun</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-03">12/03/23 03:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I first smelled this fragrance during my first winter in NYC in 2015 or '16-- coldest weather I've ever experienced in my life. I felt a warm tickle in my tummy on the first sniff and purchased immediately and wore it for the rest of the season, into the spring (in the PNW). I went on a date wearing it; he kept his face in my neck for most of night, marveling at how he couldn't get enough. I do find this scent simultaneously quite dark, sexy and bright, clean. It's easily appropriate for the office, if lightly applied, but also for an intimate night out in cooler weather. This smells exactly like an empty tea cup once full of Mariage Frères Russie Thé des Tsar with cream and honey. I used to be obsessed with drinking this tea specifically because of the wonderful "dry down" in the cup after I'd enjoyed it. It's still one of my favourites.<br />
<br />
Though I do get the fig note, the tabac note feels more prominent to me, with the fruit acting as a sweetener without going fruity or sugary.<br />
<br />
Sadly, I've only had one perfect bottle of this. Ever since that first time, now some eight years ago, every bottle I've ever purchased thereafter smells very off, cloyingly sweet and salty. I don't know if my chemistry changed, or if my taste changed, or if the formula did, but I'll always think fondly of my first bottle of Thé Noir.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1670707">L8Apex</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-10">09/10/23 16:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me predicate this my saying I am a cigar smoker, and growing up my old man smoked both pipes and cigars, and he wasn't a complete arse so I have a particular fondness for fragrances that contain a noticeable tobacco note or accord. To date I have found - and enjoy - fragrances that have sweet- or spice-oriented pipe tobacco accords, and Herod has been my go-to in this genre for five years. But this is a first for me.<br />
<br />
I know Noir 29 is supposed to be a tea scent, but the dry down is IMO the most authentic DRY tobacco leaf fragrance I have smelled to date (note: I have never smelled Mugler's Pure Havana, or SMN's Tobacco Toscano). Yes, I get the fig note. But I have encountered that *exact* same fig note in cigars and it is not uncommon to tobacco leaves (both binder and filler) from different countries. To close my eyes and take this in is to bury my nose in a well-stocked, cedar-lined humidor, or even better, to sit in a well-worn Italian leather chair in a walk-in humidor. it is the aroma of well-cured tobacco leaf at its finest.<br />
<br />
The fig note became a little more prominent on the back side of the dry down.<br />
<br />
It was only after this firsthand experience I went to see what LL said about it, as the reviews I read tend mostly to be distilled to one word: fig. And to my pleasant surprise, there it was on LL's landing page: "THÉ NOIR 29 is an ode to the noble leaf and the craft that surrounds it."<br />
<br />
Now I know they are referring to the tea leaf, but to my nose, it captures the essence of an entirely different noble leaf altogether. Maybe Tabac 28 will smell like tea to me. Or maybe I just need to smell more tea leaves. Either way, I can see adding a FB at some point in time.<br />
<br />
As other have said tho, it is not a safe blind buy; sample first.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1924758"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1924758#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1922275" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
