padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1750980">jillvee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-07">09/07/23 15:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>upon first spray onto skin and this is instantly not for me.  Maybe the heat, maybe skin chemistry but I am getting an off-putting boozy old man jack daniels alcohol vibe along w wet leaves and old potpourri. I dont get any of the opening fig or bergamot on me.  Unfortunately this is an instant scrub. I had high hopes as I've heard a lot about this but luckily I only invested in a tester.  I would say this is not a safe blind-buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1922275"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1922275#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1921960" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1921960" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mlke"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1417787"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1417787.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="mlke" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1921960ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1921960" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1417787">mlke</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-07">09/07/23 08:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I go back and forth on this a lot and am considering it as a fall purchase, but h149's reference to dollar store potpourri is a little hard to get out of my head. It's very much the unlisted rose note that I struggle with the most, although I still see the beauty of all the listed notes shining in harmony at times. I personally love the subtle hay-tobacco pairing. It feels cozy and soft in a very natural, agrestic type of way. Like you're taking a nap in some tall grasses on a cool autumn day, and the sweetness of fig comes across as ripe and jammy, but not cloyingly so, which I usually have a sensitivity to. The fruit note gives it a tender, inviting charm, and the bay leaf has a slightly green, aromatic camphor that lends a beautiful complexity to the top. It all mingles together in an alluring, almost understated smoothness. <br />
<br />
Then there's the rose- at times adding to the fruity freshness, but also recalling somewhat vintage notions of romance and dried flowers, and also veering towards soapy. In contrast, a subtle smokiness underpins most of it, but it's a sexy shade of black and gives an earthiness similar to black tea. It's here that it feels a little rougher, a little dirtier, and somewhat mysterious. It's something you want to cuddle up with in a chilly sunroom while reading a book and holding a hot drink in your hand, yet somehow the earthy, aromatic-tobacco heart feels just as appropriate to wear on a night out. One of the best Le Labo's by far, and notably something conceived outside of their usual focus on a single ingredient. Unfortunately by the end of the day I'm a little tired of the rose and doubt it's a good choice for me, but it will always have a bit of magic that keeps me wanting to try it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1921960"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1921960#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31872" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

I have of course tried your most popular fragrances and thought 'meh' but there's teeth here, I'll give you that. <br />
<br />
I can almost immediately identify this scent memory for me.  Have you ever played Manhunt/hide n seek at night, in the woods, in summer?  Crouching down in the underbrush, the thick smell of trees and loam, with that electric ozone smell in the air like fresh rain or an oncoming thunderstorm?  This is that in a bottle, and I freaking love it.  <br />
<br />
I'm so glad I took a shot on this one, I haven't purchased any from this house. Fresh, dark, clean.  I also smell rose- but its like night-blooming rose or something- sweet and dark but there.  Also feels like someone finally got tobacco right- like, seriously.  Every other house wants to slap you in the face with it so it overpowers you- this is only there in the background- very faint and just slightly sexy.  LOVE.  Also finally a unisex fragrance done right and truly unisex.  I would devour this on anyone.<br />
<br />
Forbidden rose gardens at night right before a storm.  FBW, done.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1745138"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1745138#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1739223" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A strong character. She’s not girly or flirty, she likes to be noticed in a more serious way. <br />
Update : my husband told me it smells like Jack Daniels and he loves it! Lol didn’t expect that but yay!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1428314"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1428314#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1965218" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1965218" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="spaceybailey"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1800427"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1800427.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="spaceybailey" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1965218ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1965218" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1800427">spaceybailey</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-31">10/31/23 11:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The first spray hits you with bay leaves and bergamot, but no fig. The dry down is like smoking a cigar after being in a horse barn with hay bales all around. Not In a bad way, but then again, I love being around horses. A really elegant, perfume. Gives me EQUESTRIAN girl vibes. Clean, woodsy, fresh and warm at the same time. Very unique, deep and mysterious. I love to ride horses and this perfume reminds me of that. I can see why many don't like it. It's not for just anyone. It's bold, but if layered with the right perfume it can also be gourmand. I like to layer with Kayali Eden Apple. It's like shopping for the Holidays, while drinking an apple cinnamon latte on a cold day. It gives an OUTDOORS vibe, like picking out a real tree. Kissing under the mistletoe, fresh pine cones all over your home, drinking apple punch... Like riding your horse, close to sunset, during cold weather. The smell of your black riding boots, your horse, leather saddle, your natural scent and the amazing smell of your hair, blowing as you ride away. Giving your horse an APPLE because she was such a good girl. That's what it smells like to me. I also  wear it when I'm all dressed up for a night out. I like wearing it alone but I'm a gourmand girl, so I love to layer it. This perfume is beautiful. One of my favorites from Le Labo. BISOUS</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31872"comment_id="1965218"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html?ccid=1965218#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31872" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

Sorry for the bad review but this one is not for me.  Hey, come to think of it, this is the first fragrance put out by le Labo since Estee Lauder took the company over.
